I looked at the animals across their life-span when ascribing attributes such as \""week\"" and \""strong.\"" \n\nAlso, I wasn't sure how to deal with contradictory attributes. If you say a bachelor is single, male and married, the last adjective makes the entire statement wrong even though 2 of the attributes are correct. \n\nI hope this is clear -- sorry to go on so long!
